<h5 class="kt-adv-heading79881_da0c3e-06 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_da0c3e-06">OH HI, I’M Hayley</h5>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading79881_8e774d-e0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_8e774d-e0">Welcome to my Kitchen!</h3>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79881_de9080-a5 inner-column-2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading79881_4a8145-d4 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79881_4a8145-d4">Welcome to my Kitchen!</h2>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-spacer aligncenter kt-block-spacer-79881_b4f6d2-ea"><div class="kt-block-spacer kt-block-spacer-halign-left"><hr class="kt-divider"/></div></div>



<p>Back in 2012 when I hit publish on my first blog recipe, never in a million years would I have imagined that I&#8217;d be where I am today. </p>



<p>With 2 published cookbooks;&nbsp;<a href="https://www.amazon.com/Without-Grain-Grain-Free-Gluten-Free-Wheat-Free/dp/1592336965?crid=17B5CHHUCP22B&amp;dchild=1&amp;keywords=without+grain&amp;qid=1635349035&amp;s=books&amp;sprefix=without+grain,aps,159&amp;sr=1-1&amp;linkCode=sl1&amp;tag=healstarinthe-20&amp;linkId=49e150785f6e122efada73027c719471&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow sponsored">Without Grain</a>&nbsp;&amp;&nbsp;<a href="https://www.amazon.com/Fermented-Foods-Every-Meal-Live-Culture/dp/1592337155?_encoding=UTF8&amp;qid=&amp;sr=&amp;linkCode=sl1&amp;tag=healstarinthe-20&amp;linkId=5bfd37cf9f3443ba0f118a6aff90447a&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow sponsored">Fermented Foods at Every Meal</a>&nbsp;and my recipes reaching millions of people every month, I&#8217;m beyond grateful for each and every one of you!</p>



<p>Sprinkle in a passion for food photography and I&#8217;ve finally found the secret to a successful career that doesn&#8217;t feel like work. I believe that food is the one thing that can bring us all together, it&#8217;s what we lean on during the hard times and what we use to celebrate the joys of life, so let&#8217;s make sure it&#8217;s always delicious!&nbsp;</p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

		function genesisBlocksShare( url, title, w, h ){
			var left = ( window.innerWidth / 2 )-( w / 2 );
			var top  = ( window.innerHeight / 2 )-( h / 2 );
			return window.open(url, title, 'toolbar=no, location=no, directories=no, status=no, menubar=no, scrollbars=no, resizable=no, copyhistory=no, width=600, height=600, top='+top+', left='+left);
		}
